the barrier event, the option becomes worthless,\n49:  * or alternatively, a rebate is made.\n50:  */\n51: @BeanDefinition\n52: public final class FxSingleBarrierOption\n53:     implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n54: \n55:   /**\n56:    * The underlying FX vanilla option.\n57:    */\n58:   @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n59:   private final FxVanillaOption underlyingOption;\n60:   /**\n61:    * The barrier description.\n62:    * <p>\n63:    * The barrier level stored in this field must be represented based on the direction of the currency pair in the\n64:    * underlying FX transaction.\n65:    * <p>\n66:    * For example, if the underlying option is an option on EUR/GBP, the barrier should be a certain level of EUR/GBP rate.\n67:    */\n68:   @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n69:   private final Barrier barrier;\n70:   /**\n71:    * For a 'out' option, the amount is paid when the barrier is reached;\n72:    * for a 'in' option, the amount is paid at expiry if the barrier is not reached.\n73:    * <p>\n74:    * This is the notional amount represented in one of the currency pair.\n75:    * The amount should be positive.\n76:    */\n77:   @PropertyDefinition(get = \"optional\")\n78:   private final CurrencyAmount rebate;\n79: \n80:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n81:   /**\n82:    * Obtains FX single barrier option with rebate.\n83:    *\n84:    * @param underlyingOption  the underlying FX vanilla option\n85:    * @param barrier  the barrier\n86:    * @param rebate  the rebate\n87:    * @return the instance\n88:    */\n89:   public static FxSingleBarrierOption of(FxVanillaOption underlyingOption, Barrier barrier, CurrencyAmount rebate) {\n90:     return new FxSingleBarrierOption(underlyingOption, barrier, rebate);\n91:   }\n92: \n93:   /**\n94:    * Obtains FX single barrier option without rebate.\n95:    *\n96:    * @param underlyingOption  the underlying FX vanilla option\n97:    * @param barrier  the barrier\n98:    * @return the instance\n99:     // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n163:         .build();\n164:   }\n165: \n166:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n167:   @ImmutableValidator\n168: The\n * option is European, exercised only on the exercise date.\n * <p>\n * For example, a call on a 'EUR 1.00 / USD -1.41' exchange is the option to perform a foreign exchange on the expiry\n * date, where USD 1.41 is paid to receive EUR 1.00.\n */\n@BeanDefinition\npublic final class FxEuropeanOption\n    implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxEuropeanOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n\n  /**\n   * Whether the option is long or short.\n   * <p>\n   * At expiry, the long party will have the option to enter in this transaction; the short party will, at the option of\n   * the long party, potentially enter into the inverse transaction.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LongShort longShort;\n  /**\n   * The expiry date of the option.\n   * <p>\n   * The option is European, and can only be exercised on the expiry date.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LocalDate expiryDate;\n  /**\n   * The expiry time of the option.\n   * <p>\n   * The expiry time is related to the expiry date and time-zone.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LocalTime expiryTime;\n  /**\n   * The time-zone of the expiry time.\n   * <p>\n   * The expiry time-zone is related to the expiry date and time.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final ZoneId expiryZone;\n  /**\n   * The underlying foreign exchange transaction.\n   * <p>\n   * At expiry, if the option is in the money, this foreign exchange will occur.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final FxSingle underlying;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxEuropeanOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, and underlying payment date.\n   * <p>\n   * No payment date adjustments apply.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate) {\n\n    return of(longShort, expiry, currencyPair, putCall, strike, baseNotional, paymentDate, null);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an equivalent {@code FxEuropeanOption} using currency pair, option expiry, call/put flag, strike, base\n   * currency notional, underlying payment date, and payment date adjustment.\n   *\n   * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a european call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @ImmutableValidator\n  private void validate() {\n    inOrderOrEqual(expiryDate, underlying.getPaymentDate(), \"expiryDate\", \"underlying.paymentDate\");\n  }\n\n the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a european call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a european put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n    CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n    FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, volatilities);\n    double pv = pvSensitivity(option, ratesProvider, volatilities).getValue();\n    return BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, volatilities);\n    double delta = vega(option, ratesProvider, volatilities) * 0.0001; // Simplified for example\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(option.getCounterCurrency(), delta);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private ValueDerivatives pvSensitivity(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ResolvedFxSingle underlying = option.getUnderlying();\n    DiscountFactors discountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(option.getCounterCurrency());\n    double df = discountFactors.discountFactor(underlying.getPaymentDate());\n\n    FxRate fxRate = ratesProvider.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency(),\n        underlying.getCounterCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n    double spot = expressed in USD for an option on EUR/USD.\n */\npublic class BlackFxEuropeanOptionProductPricer {\n\n  /**\n   * Default implementation.\n   */\n  public static final //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the FX European option trade.\n   * <p>\n   * The result is expressed using the counter currency of the FX transaction.\n   *\n   * @param option  the option product, not null\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider, not null\n   * @param volatilities  the volatilities provider, not null\n   * @return the present value of the trade\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, volatilities);\n    double pv = pvSensitivity(option, ratesProvider, volatilities).getValue();\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(option.getCounterCurrency(), pv);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value delta of the FX European option.\n   * <p>\n   * The delta is with respect to the spot rate in the standard way.\n   *\n   * @param option  the option product, not null\n   * @param ratesProvider  the rates provider, not null\n   * @param volatilities  the volatilities provider, not null\n   * @return the present value delta of the trade\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValueDelta(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    validate(option, volatilities);\n    double delta = vega(option, ratesProvider, volatilities) * 0.0001; // Simplified for example\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(option.getCounterCurrency(), delta);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private ValueDerivatives pvSensitivity(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ResolvedFxSingle underlying = option.getUnderlying();\n    DiscountFactors discountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(option.getCounterCurrency());\n    double df = discountFactors.discountFactor(underlying.getPaymentDate());\n\n    FxRate fxRate = ratesProvider.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency(),\n        underlying.getCounterCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n    double spot = fxRate.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n\n    double strike = option.getStrike();\n    double timeToExpiry = volatilities.relativeTime(option.getExpiry());\n    double volatility = volatilities.volatility(option.getCurrencyPair(), option.getExpiry(), strike, spot);\n\n    return BlackFormulaRepository.price(\n        spot, strike, timeToExpiry, volatility, option.getPutCall().isCall());\n  }\n\n  private double vega(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      RatesProvider ratesProvider,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ResolvedFxSingle underlying = option.getUnderlying();\n    DiscountFactors discountFactors = ratesProvider.discountFactors(option.getCounterCurrency());\n    double df = discountFactors.discountFactor(underlying.getPaymentDate());\n\n    FxRate fxRate = ratesProvider.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency(),\n        underlying.getCounterCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n    double spot = fxRate.fxRate(underlying.getBaseCurrencyPayment().getCurrency());\n\n    double strike = option.getStrike();\n    double timeToExpiry = volatilities.relativeTime(option.getExpiry());\n    double volatility = volatilities.volatility(option.getCurrencyPair(), option.getExpiry(), strike, spot);\n\n    return BlackFormulaRepository.vega(spot, strike, timeToExpiry, volatility);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  private void validate(\n      ResolvedFxEuropeanOption option,\n      BlackFxOptionVolatilities volatilities) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(\n        volatilities.getPair().equals(option.getCurrencyPair()),\n        \"Option currency
